          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.013)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (mlp): Mlp(
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
      (2): SelfAttentionBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): SelfAttention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.025)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (mlp): Mlp(
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
      (3): SelfAttentionBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): SelfAttention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.038)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (mlp): Mlp(
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
      (4): SelfAttentionBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): SelfAttention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.050)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (mlp): Mlp(
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
      (5): SelfAttentionBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): SelfAttention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.062)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (mlp): Mlp(
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
      (6): SelfAttentionBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): SelfAttention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)

        (mlp): Mlp(

        )
      )
      (7): SelfAttentionBlock(
        (norm1): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): SelfAttention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.087)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
    )
    (z_untied_pos_enc): Untied2DPositionalEncoder(
      (pos): Learned2DPositionalEncoder()
      (norm): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (pos_q_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (pos_k_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
    )
    (x_untied_pos_enc): Untied2DPositionalEncoder(
      (pos): Learned2DPositionalEncoder()
      (norm): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (pos_q_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (pos_k_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
    )
    (rpe_bias_table): RelativePosition2DEncoder()
  )
  (decoder): ConcatenationBasedDecoder(
    (layers): ModuleList(
      (0): CrossAttentionBlock(
        (norm1_q): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm1_kv): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): CrossAttention(
          (q): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (kv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1024, bias=True)
          (attn_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (proj_drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
        (drop_path): DropPath(drop_prob=0.100)
        (norm2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (mlp): Mlp(
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2048, bias=True)
          (act): GELU(approximate='none')
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
          (drop): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
        )
      )
    )
    (z_untied_pos_enc): Untied2DPositionalEncoder(
      (pos): Learned2DPositionalEncoder()
      (norm): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (pos_k_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
    )
    (x_untied_pos_enc): Untied2DPositionalEncoder(
      (pos): Learned2DPositionalEncoder()
      (norm): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (pos_q_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (pos_k_linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
    )
    (rpe_bias_table): RelativePosition2DEncoder()
  )
  (out_norm): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (head): MlpHead(
    (cls_mlp): Mlp(
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0-1): 2 x Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1, bias=True)
      )
      (act): GELU(approximate='none')
      (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
    )
    (reg_mlp): Mlp(
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0-1): 2 x Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=4, bias=True)
      )
      (act): GELU(approximate='none')
      (drop): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
    )
  )
)
